        .image-placeholder {

--- info-agentica.md ---
## Agentica AI Overview

**Founder:** Moudy

### Key Points
- Agentica AI likely focuses on AI agents for businesses, aiming to boost efficiency.
- Offers services like 24/7 support and integration with tools such as Slack.
- Recent activity suggests engagement in early 2025, but founding date and funding details remain unclear.

### Company Mission and Services
Agentica AI specializes in AI solutions for businesses, particularly enhancing operational efficiency through domain-specific AI agents. Their mission is to deploy AI trained on business workflows to create, standardize, and integrate AI, enabling a 10x increase in operational efficiency and strategic growth.

**Core Services:**
- **Intelligence Hubâ„¢:** Converts tribal knowledge into operational intelligence.
- **AI Agents:** Domain-trained experts available from day one.
- **Reasoning Engine:** Expert-level AI reasoning for business operations.
- **Dynamic Workflows:** Converts static documentation into Infrastructure as Code (IaC), improving workflow automation.
- **Security & Compliance:** Comprehensive monitoring, logging, and auditing.
- **Structured Input/Output:** Uses structured Markdown files for workflow automation.
- **Seamless Tool Integration:** API support for Dropbox, Microsoft Teams, Trello, Jira, GitHub, Google Drive, Gmail, and more.
- **Enterprise-Grade Security:** Bank-level security, automated compliance, and audit trails.
- **Rapid Deployment:** Integrates with ServiceNow, Slack, and other enterprise tools with minimal disruption.

A key feature is **Milo**, an AI teammate that provides 24/7 support, automating routine tasks to reduce burnout and increase productivity. The platform is particularly focused on addressing tech operations challenges, including DevOps talent shortages and security breaches caused by human error.

### Market Context & Industry Challenges
- 67% of IT leaders struggle to find qualified DevOps talent.
- 80% of security breaches stem from human error.
- Engineers spend 30% of their time researching solutions.
- Critical incidents often occur outside business hours.
- The platform extends a technology team's productivity by 10x.

### Recent Activity
Agentica AI has been active on LinkedIn, sharing AI-related articles and insights in early 2025. Topics include:
- The role of AI in redefining engineering velocity.
- AI startup strategies and leadership insights.
- Global AI developments, such as DeepSeek AI surpassing ChatGPT.
- OpenAI's Operator mode launch for ChatGPT Pro users.

### Gaps in Information
- Founding date and funding details are not publicly available.
- The company is not listed on Crunchbase or PitchBook under "Agentica AI."
- Speculated to be recently established based on 2025 activity.

### Conclusion
Agentica AI is an emerging player in AI-driven business automation, offering seamless enterprise integration and a strong focus on security and efficiency. While their solutions present significant advantages, the lack of transparency regarding their founding details and funding remains a notable gap.

2022 ANNUAL REPORT

POWERING GROWTH.
EXPANDING POSSIBILITIES.
At SGH, we design and manufacture 
technologies that support and advance 
our world. Across computing, memory, 
and LED lighting solutions, we are focused 
on serving customers in specialty end 
markets by providing advanced technical 
expertise, custom design engineering, 
build to order flexibility, and a commitment 
to best in class quality. At SGH, we 
continue to invest in our future with the 
goal of delivering sustainable growth and 
lasting results.
1 SGH   2022 Annual Report

Intelligent Platform Solutions (IPS)
Our IPS group offers specialized platform solutions 
and services for high-performance computing 
(HPC), artificial intelligence (AI), machine learning 
(ML), advanced modeling, and the internet of 
things (IoT) that span the continuum of edge, core, 
and cloud. Our solutions are designed specifically 
for customers across government, hyperscale, 
energy, financial services, and education markets.
Memory Solutions
Our Memory Solutions group delivers high-
performance memory solutions through the 
design, development, and advanced packaging 
of leading-edge products. These specialty 
memory products meet customer-specific 
requirements across a broad spectrum of markets, 
including networking and communications, 
enterprise storage, desktop, notebook and server 
applications, smartphones, and others.
LED Solutions
Our LED Solutions group provides application-
optimized LED chips and components for high 
power and mid-power general lighting, video 
screens, and specialty lighting applications leading 
the industry in performance and reliability. 
3 SGH   2022 Annual Report 2OUR BUSINESS LINES
Since our inception over 30 
years ago, SGH has grown into 
a diversified group of business 
lines focused on the design 
and manufacture of specialty 
solutions for the computing, 
memory, and LED markets.

7 SGH   2022 Annual Report 6DEAR SGH SHAREHOLDERS, 
During my two years as CEO, my team and I have been leading 
the companyâ€™s transformation into a more diversified business 
that strives to deliver long term growth and profitability. SGH 
achieved record financial results in Fiscal 2022 while continuing 
on our journey to build a world-class company. Guided by a focus 
to support our valued customers, we continue to invest in people, 
innovation, and operational excellence as we look to power growth 
and expand possibilities. 
In FY 2022, we achieved record revenues, gross margins, 
and non-GAAP earnings per share (EPS). Our efforts to 
create a high-performance culture anchored in shared 
purpose and core values were recognized by the Great 
Place to WorkÂ® Institute, which certified SGH as a Great 
Place to Work.
We produced these results despite persistent 
geopolitical and macroeconomic uncertainty. T ogether 
with the SGH team, we maintained our focus on results 
and delivered:
  Record overall annual revenue of $1.8 billion (a 21% 
increase from FY 2021) from our three business lines:
â€¢  Intelligent Platform Solutions,  which brought 
in a record $441 million in FY 2022 (a 28% increase 
from FY 2021)
â€¢  Memory Solutions , which earned $975 million in 
FY 2022 (a 5% increase from FY 2021)â€¢  LED Solutions, our newest business line, which 
added approximately $403 million in revenue 
during FY 2022
  Record annual gross margin of 24.9% (an increase 
of 440 basis points year-over-year), with non-GAAP 
gross margin of 25.9% (an increase of 370 basis 
points year-over-year)
  Record annual adjusted EBITDA of $263 million, an 
exceptional 40% increase over FY 2021
  Record non-GAAP earnings of $3.62 per share in 
FY 2022 (compared to $2.61 in FY 2021)
Shortly after the end of FY 2022, we closed the 
acquisition of Stratus Technologies, a leading provider 
of advanced high-availability and fault-tolerant 
computing platforms, software, and services. This new addition to SGH builds on our solid M&A track 
record and further demonstrates our commitment to 
growth through diversification. 
Alongside our financial performance, we worked to live 
up to our responsibilities as a corporate citizen and 
employer. In our most recent ESG report, released in 
October 2022, we outlined the steps we are taking to 
make a positive impact both within our business and in 
the communities where our employees, customers, and 
partners live and work. More specifically: 
ENVIRONMENT
We recognize the ongoing threat of climate 
change and understand that we have a 
responsibility to minimize environmental 
impact throughout our operations and value 
chain. This year we committed to achieving 
net-zero Scope 1 and Scope 2 carbon 
emissions by 2030.
DIVERSITY, EQUITY, AND INCLUSION 
At SGH, we understand the importance of a 
diverse and engaged workforce. Our gender 
diversity worldwide improved, with the 
proportion of woman employees rising from 
41% to 45%. We also conducted a pay parity 
analysis to inform our efforts to advance pay 
equity within SGH. 
GOVERNANCE
We increased executive accountability 
and formally introduced ESG oversight as a 
chartered responsibility of the Nominating 
and Corporate Governance Committee of 
the Board of Directors. Starting in 2023, we 
will include measurable ESG performance 
goals in our executive bonus program in 
order to hold our executives accountable for 
progress on ESG issues.On behalf of our worldwide employees, I want to thank 
you, our shareholders, for your continued support. I am 
proud to lead the SGH team and excited for the future 
we have together.
Sincerely,
Mark Adams  
Chief Executive Officer
